    2556             :     ! getTranGaus    Pseudorandom numbers from a truncated Gaussian distribution.
    2557             :     !
    2558             :     !   X = getTranGaus(lowerLim,B) returns a pseudorandom variable generated from a normal
    2559             :     !   distribution with mean zero and standard deviation one (i.e. standard
    2560             :     !   normal distribution) truncated to the interval [lowerLim,B].
    2561             :     !

    2563             :     !   a normal distribution with mean avg and standard deviation std
    2564             :     !   truncated to the interval [lowerLim,B].
    2565             :     !
